### Document type ? Defined by: - a unique name - an optional super Document Type  - a set of schemas  - Define storage structure  - a set of facets  -Define document behavior or capabilities 
### Schemas - A schema is a set of different fields  - Each field has:  - A name  - A type  - Common types are: - string - int - float - date - blob (complex) - complex

### Reusable schemas - reusable by several doc types - Studio creates a schema for each doc type - can technically be reused - from Nuxeo: - dublincore - common - uid - file - files See nxserver/schemas
### Document type with extension points Contributing new schemas Contributing a new Document Type 
# Exercise - Document types ######Sun Seng David TAN - Thomas ROGER
### Connect ... - Create a trial account and access Nuxeo Studio [https://connect.nuxeo.com/nuxeo/site/connect/trial/form](https://connect.nuxeo.com/nuxeo/site/connect/trial/form) - Download (if not already done) a Nuxeo server and install it on your computer [http://www.nuxeo.com/fr/telechargez-nuxeo](http://www.nuxeo.com/fr/telechargez-nuxeo)  - Install the Nuxeo DM module and keep the default settings. 
### Book library - We want to manage books  - Define a new Book Document type - Define a new schema containing the required fields  - Register our new document type
### What fields do we need? - Let’s say that, for now, a Book is defined by:  - Its ISBN (string)  - Its author (string)  - Its publicationDate (date)  - A rating (int)
### Try out your changes - Start your Nuxeo DM server  - In Nuxeo DM, go to the Admin Center  - Connect to the admin center  - Register your instance of Nuxeo DM  - Synchronize your Nuxeo Studio configuration with Nuxeo DM (Update center → nuxeo studio → update)  - Create new Book documents in Nuxeo
## Thank you!
